[33mMd[39m(e[33m,[39mt[33m,[39mr){[36mlet[39m n[33m=[39me[33m.[39mtype[33m;[39m[36mswitch[39m(n){[36mcase[39m[32m"parameter"[39m[33m:[39m[36mreturn[39m
